                                   31695              Ÿ  XCMDSCAN - SCAN FOR SPECIAL EXEC STATEMENTS (COMMANDS)             Ÿ
                                   31696              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   31697              Ÿ  WE SCAN FOR THE FOLLOWING SPECIAL EXEC STATMENTS:                  Ÿ
                                   31698              Ÿ       1. ASSIGNMENT, INDICATED BY <VAR> = ...                       Ÿ
                                   31699              Ÿ       2. LABEL, INDICATED BY <LABEL VAR>: ...                       Ÿ
                                   31700              Ÿ       3. ARRAY ASSIGNMENT, INDICATED BY <ARRAY NAME>[ ...           Ÿ
                                   31701              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   31702              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   31703              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                   31704              Ÿ       SCAN CONTROL BLOCK POINTS TO COMMAND                          Ÿ
                                   31705              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   31706              Ÿ  ON EXIT:                                                           Ÿ
                                   31707              Ÿ       1. IF LINE IS SPECICAL EXEC STATMENT,  WE CALL PROCESSING     Ÿ
                                   31708              Ÿ          THE APPROPRIATE PROCESSING ROUTINE.  WE DO NOT RETURN.     Ÿ
                                   31709              Ÿ       2. IF THE LINE IS NOT SPECIAL EXEC STATEMENT,,, WE JUST       Ÿ
                                   31710              Ÿ          RETURN                                                     Ÿ
                                   31711              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
